Breakfast is relatively small and beautiful, the rice noodles are delicious, and there is also a very special oil tea to experience, because it is small. The waiters remember you and will greet you

Service: The staff of this hotel are all very good and warm. I feel that Haitang Bay Crown is not so considerate. The room I booked for my family may be a bit noisy, and they also suggested that we change to a lower-priced room üòÇ, which is also very practical. The bed guard, baby chair and stroller are also prepared and provided. Don't bring children too convenient

The hotel also provides airport pick-up service. On the first day, the flight was delayed and arrived very late. The pick-up master did not complain, and took us to find several convenience stores to buy fresh milk for the little friends. I felt that the people here were too good on the first night in Guilin

Geographic location: It is very centrally located, not far from the Li River, Elephant Trunk Hill and the pier are within walking distance, and it is also very convenient to eat and buy medicine around. It is a little far from the airport.

The only drawback is that the hotel's soundproofing is not particularly good. The noise from the corridor and the sound of traffic outside the window may have some impact on people who have trouble sleeping. However, the advantages outweigh the disadvantages. The price-performance ratio is very high. If I come to Guilin next time, I will stay here again.

It turned out that this bus picked up people everywhere. The cruise only lasted an hour before we were taken ashore. The tour guide took us to a small village on the shore for lunch, and then took a bus (note that it was a bus, not a cruise ship) to the so-called ethnic minority village they promoted, a so-called The Dong village is actually a man-made village where silverware is sold, which is said to be purely handmade. When we entered, we were treated to a show of manipulation, such as an old Dong grandmother, a national treasure, etc. After a while, I realized that it was a place selling silverware. The tourists on our bus were very angry at that time and asked the tour guide why traveling on the Li River turned into taking a bus. We agreed to arrive in Yangshuo before 5 pm, but we arrived in Yangshuo County at 8 pm.
